Gradually, enlightenment dawns,
The four seasons revealed—
How to pluck and refine them?
Gradually, the years slip by in an instant.

Gradually, the Daoist landscape emerges,
Worthy of summoning and embracing.
Gradually, qi and spirit are refined,
Transformed into elixir—
Ever more harmonized.

Gradually, the path ahead unfolds,
Clearly marked—
Clouds part beneath my tread.
No longer bound,
The Dao’s virtue/power ascends.

---
**迎春乐春日**
At dawn, auspicious qi stirs—
Spring’s warmth arrives early.
The mud ox reveals itself—
Ancient Farmer Cao’s omen.
With a graceful jade staff,
Who compares to me,
The Revere-the-Aged Daoist?

Feasting on treasures held close,
Savoring broad meals of herbs.
Already permitted to forge the elixir,
Returning to Penglai Isle.

---
**曾梅春#3**
Amid the dusty world,
All vie for beauty’s fleeting grace.
Displaying pearls and gold,
Silks and brocades—
Emotions woven in embroidery.
Children, wives, all gather together,
Music and dance in timely pursuit.
No rest—
Last night, tonight,
Endless layers of delay.
How often do they pause,
To turn back and awaken?
Only when the Dark Lord arrives,
Will their guilt truly tremble.
A thousand sorrowful expressions,
A hundred grievous thoughts—
Brows knit like blades.
Seeing the summons,
This regret now,
Cannot be concealed.

---
**凤栖梧**
By nature, I seek stillness,
Claiming the path of clouds and waters,
Endless wanderings.
Polished pearls are washed again,
Constellations rekindled—
Their hues freshly carved.
Whether seated or roaming,
In stillness, I know—
There is one who seeks me.
Often, I meet with golden dew,
Steadfast on Penglai’s path.

---
**茶瓶儿**
First, filial piety to the Golden Mother,
No power to abandon father or seek parent.
Daily offerings in baskets and trays,
Recognizing my own ancestral roots.
Call to my children—
Ride dragons and tigers,
Now is the time to serve the Divine.
Awake and reverent,
Returning to the Purple Palace,
Recording names in the Celestial Ledger.

---
**柳梢青**
Naturally refined—
Rice’s essence, wheat’s marrow.
Who can fathom
The secrets I know?
Nurturing harmony,
Enhancing wisdom,
With spirit-water’s aid.
Three luminaries’ radiance spreads,
Aiding the True Yang’s origin.
Forging the elixir,
Brightly returning to the Primordial Home.

---
**解佩令**
The Golden Lad, sleek and polished,
The Jade Maiden, slender and graceful.
Worthy of shared longevity—
Both at twenty-eight.
Where do they dwell?
One by the water, one in the northern mountains,
Entering the *Li* gate, the *Kan* door—
All are perilous.
Frequently they pull and search,
Street after street,
Every quarter reached.

**寻得灵珠**
Found the spirit pearl,
With elixir nectar and spirit-water anointed,
Radiant with myriad luminous whirls.

The Wind King’s harm—three times before,
He cut taxes in advance.
For love of wine, he drowned in drink.
Coming and going, past events forgotten,
Falling asleep in the street like a virtuous man.
Armpit cloths and headkerchiefs all abandoned.
There are scriptures with hidden precepts within.
Deep gratitude to the enlightened sage,
Who, with benevolent heart, lifts them with me—
*解佩令*—repaying the worthy’s goodwill.

At the willow pavilion, land deeds placed,
Buying floating mulberry groves.
On the Penglai path, coolness made.
Gradually, efficacy takes hold—
On Kunlun’s heights, auspicious signs arise.
Each island opens three gates,
With nine named halls of distinction.
Gradually, the Primordial Void’s silent origin emerges,
Then the gathered essence reveals the Original Yang.
Passing through the Hall of Clarity,
Gazing at the blazing scene—
Here, neighboring brilliance shines forth.
Residing here, now settled,
Dwelling in the immortal’s Penglai isle—
Spring’s essence refined, flowers and grasses fresh.
Summer’s heat blooms the red lotus.
Suddenly, autumn arrives early,
And cicadas sing in the willow pavilion.
A gale brings the northern wind,
Scattering white snow across the valleys.
A hundred years’ time like a flick of the fingers—
One true spirit, searching for profound mysteries.
Afterward, all is complete.
Nurturing harmony of spirit and qi,
Forging the radiant elixir into a perfect sphere.
The Five Paths gleam together,
Escorting ascent to the Great Luo Heaven.
By nature, compassionate—
Seeking the Mysterious Mechanism.
Wondrous principles ascend,
Desiring to ponder.
The body cannot escape—
Driven by the fires of familial bonds.
Love and desire fiercely abandoned,
Yet how to leave wife and children behind?
This elixir, once formed, splits in two—
If forced to act or rest, it follows inevitably.
But fear not its control.
Both halves united, all learn the Way of Non-Action.
At the end of stillness, each finds their place—
Only Master Pang knows this.

**耍蛾儿**
Not knowing how to cultivate—
Just nurturing an empty belly,
Kidneys, lungs, heart, liver, spleen—
Five clumps of foul flesh—what master are they?
First, drive away the Yellow Woman.
Confront the Azure Dragon and White Tiger,
No need for infants or maidens.
Gentlemen seeking the path of longevity—
There is another gate.
If one knows how to cultivate and seek the swift path,
The Full Reality’s gate opens wide.
Mercury knows Lead as its ancestor,
Securing the essence to halt the vital breath.
Even the inverted yin-yang numbers—
Today, clearly explained.
Depend on these four characters,
And soon you’ll return to the Dao.

**七骑子**
Truly, Master Zhongyang,
Met with a fortunate cause.
The cause awaits fulfillment—
Cultivate the Dao, become an immortal.
The immortals are awake and sincere—
The elixir’s single round pearl complete.
Auspicious clouds bear it to Heaven.
The Heavenly Master grants the White Flower Lotus.
The Lotus gleams most brightly,
Freshest, most radiant—
Radiant and fragrant, wondrous and profound.
Ascending to the Jade Emperor’s presence.
Leisurely steps drift—
Beyond the western suburbs.
Seeing skeletons lie,
Lying on the sandbank.
Ask why your fate is thus—
For love of children, wife, and kin.
Now suffering bitter wine.
Eyes grow sores, mouths fill with dust.
Qi chokes—cannot exhale,
Exhaling only rainbows.
Rain and wind scatter all—
Mostly, children trample them.
Regretting no good deeds in life.

---
*(End of Volume Eleven of Zhongyang’s Full Reality Collection)*
#1 This tune should be *"Golden Man Holding the Dew Tray."*
#2 This tune should be *"Duoli."*
#3 This tune should be *"Snow Plum Fragrance."*

**迎仙客**
To greet the Celestial Guest—
Practice must be sought with care,
True stillness, true clarity, true heart must be found.
This side verdant, that side white,
A head of black, a crown of crimson bright.
Together they dwell in halls of lapis,
Jade-petal blossoms bloom with crushed crystal dew.
Jade boys sing, golden boys clap—
Heaven’s choice has fallen upon the Guest.
This tune’s break, the first break enters—
The Guest’s place knows no break.
Examined, understood—
See how it splits my belly wide.
How does one do it? Just so—
Why sleep through the *ziwu* hours?
What’s said, what’s taught—
Self-wrapped in darkness, alone in practice.
This *haifeng* wind—my heart is broken,
A sudden end to this strange discipline.
No calamity, no disaster—
No seeking, no grasping, no ink-stained scholar’s fate.
Great Immortals chant, True Ones respond—
In the Full Reality Hall, no smoke, no flame.
Wu-you Child, with three companions,
Instantly cool, at ease, seated in freedom.

---

**香山会**
White radiance blooms with emerald hue,
Red splendor gathers in perfection.
Mysterious yellow shines with celestial depth—
Layer upon layer, pearls draped in splendor.
Through boundless skies, Daoists come and go.
Sealed with eternal title, now the Jade Emperor’s decree is received.
Within clouds and mists, the True Ones ascend.
At the Fragrant Mountain Gathering, pearly words unfold the Way.
Together they return to dwell forever in the Three Isles.

---

**红芍药**
Only when one is fully awake
Can one boast of true perfection.
Clear messages are seen—
Now the perfect midday sleep is taken.
This *ziwu* hour compels the spirit’s flow,
The Bottle Constellation—how could it be ignored?
When the Jade Door opens, lock the Golden Pass.
Lock the Golden Pass—
Never meet with lustful winds,
Nor fall to the fires of karma.
The Six Realms’ wheel is utterly avoided.
Free and unbound—
Above and below, white qi fills the void,
A single elixir grain, forged into gold.
From the sky, celestial music welcomes,
Heavenly flowers bloom in perfect order.

---

**塞孤**
My voice alone—who could measure it?
A maiden with green face, white limbs—
Stone Girl comes to respond.
Slender her form, her waist like a jade flute,
Soft and yielding, dancing in graceful sway,
Gold mirrors and pearl strings all at her command.
Let all be fulfilled, repay this merit.
At first scent of jade blossom’s fragrance,
It is the crystal flower crushed.
Two segments of moss, the same hue—
Even the Spirit Boys are ordered to pluck.
Together they meet—worthy of pity,
Displaying wonders beyond measure.
Rising above the Azure Han,
She gazes clearly.
With new melodies, forever as a Celestial Guest.

---

**双雁儿**
I urge you to the Western Realm—
Cast off restraint, wander as clouds.
Then you shall know no sorrow.
This worry fades, little by little.
Slowly, pull back the six oxen.
Recognize the waters, the grasses—
Your body becomes pure white through true cultivation.
Ascend in freedom, the boat reaches shore.

---
**自述**
The mind-horse, heart-monkey—do not let them stray.
The *haifeng* wind bears my name: Wang Zhe.
Since my heart broke, I’ve been turned upside down.
Fearful of dissipating old karma.
True nature, true spirit—what more is there to say?
Like dawn’s wind, the moon’s last light.
At the Yang Willow Ravine, all is clear.
I pluck at will.

---
**愍郭郎**
The Dao’s leisure is its own perfection—
A carefree little Immortal.

**《谨修增些福》**
I earnestly cultivate to increase some **virtue/power**—
Descend into the Yellow Spring.

**Foolish and bewildered**, I know nothing at all,
Only love a few coins of money.
When the great limit arrives one day,
I shall lament to the Azure Sky.

**Lost in delusion**, I follow the **Dao/Way**;
At leisure, I wander without hindrance.
Gazing alone at the brocade waves of the **Jinbo**,
And the verdant peaks of the **Qingdai**.

Turning back, I suddenly see beyond the desolate woods—
A heap of skulls lying, tangled in the reeds.
Who now owns this lone, pitiful place?
They are all **sorting** together.

My hollow eyes are filled with dust—
Earthly particles block my sight.
Rain washes, wind blows, sun scorches—
Stars shine in silent opposition.

For **karmic transformation**, I add layer upon layer,
Heavily burdened anew.
In strange lands and distant realms,
Where am I a guest? What age?

The shepherd boy arrives,
Frequently striking with his staff,
Desiring to scatter them.
In past lives, I coveted wealth and lust,
And clung to love.

**Lost in delusion**, how can I escape?
The **Hongchuang** tune—
**Liu Yue’s Dao/Way** is sincere and potent.
At the **Equal Community**, some recognize, others do not.

This is the **root of virtue/power**,
For the sake of **tranquility and benefit**.
I wish you would soon accumulate **auspicious causes**.
Seek the **Dao/Way** within your heart.

If you boast, you’ll topple like a balanced scale—
Do not let even a drop slip away.
Grind ink with a wooden slab and broken tile.
Before my window, the bamboo—
I see its true **effortless grace**.

Ask those who **skillfully point the tea**—
Who can truly **walk the Dao/Way**?
**Compassion and mercy** must not be abandoned.
Do good deeds by striking the cup—
Why wait for a silent sound?

Ask those who **abide in freedom and ease**—
How does **accumulating virtue** attain this?
Their appearance is pleasing,
Worthy of my likeness.
Empty hands, empty words—
The **Dao/Way** is broken, the home abandoned.

They can store thin vinegar, salt, and pickled greens,
Dried vegetables turned into fermented pastes.
I entrust them to **Zhang Gong**—
Steady and firm in your grasp.
Do not let them slip,
Crushed beneath your feet.
A hundred fragments, piece by piece,
Scattered when the time comes.

**Seventy-three, thirty-seven**—
At that moment, ponder **Wang Ji, Wang Ji**.
The cliffside is perilous, yet firm—
But guard against losing your footing.

I urge you to turn back, not to cling.
The **headwrap** remains only until
Next year’s New Year’s Day.
If you persist as before—
**Mind-horse, heart-monkey**—
Your lifespan will reach ninety.

But as a mortal, you must rely on **virtue/power**.
Do not scorn heaven or slight the earth—
Clothing and food will suffice.

This very night, however,
There is a **Wang San**, alone with his parents.
No comings or goings, no blankets or quilts.
Sleeping in his clothes, still and serene,
He will not stir or be disturbed.

When he wakes, he feels even more **cool and refreshed**,
Speaking only of poetry and melodies.
By next year, he will be **ripe with wisdom**.
This **lofty peak of the heart** remains unlit—
Unfathomable **kalpas** of waves,
Greedily grasping fame and fortune.
The earth turns to gold, yet it is still insufficient.

Why then do you not **plant good causes**,
For a better rebirth?
Do you not know that **two by two, three by three**,
We see **five by five, six by six**?
To honor **brother and sister-in-law**,
To provide **auspicious offerings**.

Even now, these are my **living parents**—
Who dares to face them?
But here, there is **Wang San**,
Whom I think of morning and evening.
Brother and sister-in-law, do not grieve or sigh.
Do not worry—
Purify your heart with **sincere reflection**.
The **fragrance of fame** is fleeting—
All three teachings **observe** it,
Yet **virtuous growth** flourishes.

This **Wang San** is **worthy of competition**.
He has extinguished **greed for wealth and lust**,
And wandered in the **threefold bliss of desire**.
Why then do you not **cease offering incense and wine**?
Even the **Immortal** loves this.

**Walking alone**, he is truly **free and at ease**.
To **conceal everywhere**, to **banish all demons**.
Many **heart sutras**, remembered clearly—
**No obstruction, no hindrance**.

**Wang Zhe**—
From my beginning, I have had **some offerings**.
I have had **some offerings**.

「The **Dao** is held daily with diligence,
Searching for hidden precepts.

The **Underworld** does not dare to glance.
In the **Heavenly Realm**, one naturally rejoices.
The **Penglai Immortal**’s island is like returning home,
And **cultivation** is fully realized.

*Wang Zhe* fears not the **harmful winds**—he cares nothing for them.
He delights in leisure, indulging in **effortless ease** and **indolence**.

A **paper robe** and **hempen clothes**—
Let others speak of their shortcomings,
For I know my own **coolness and warmth**.

A single **incense stick**’s worth of fame,
And ten **volumes** of **scripture**—
Three thousand **days** of **meritorious practice**,
And **fulfillment** is complete.

Steadily guiding the **auspicious clouds**,
Alone traversing the **Celestial Paths**,
Let him race the *Wang Zhe*’s **night-voyaging boat**.

#*Water Clouds Wandering*— **Equality, equality**.

Returning to **Laizhou**,
One must **rescue and deliver**.

The **harmful winds**—
**Transformation** is evenly distributed,
And those **transformed for the good** willingly return to **virtue**.

The **Two Principles** and **Three Radiances** are always upright.
**Examining** a person’s heart is like weighing with a **square scale**.

If not **highly elevated**, one sinks into **lowliness**—
Even the **Immortal** has **retribution**.

*Small Heavy Mountain*—
**Worthy of lamentation**, the calf, **worthy of lamentation**, the ox.
If you still **overlook** my words,
You are **of the same stream**.

**Nature** is like a **lamp**, **fate** like **oil**.
Mutual **nurturing** and **kindling**,
Flame **radiates**, illuminating the **mountain’s light**.

It **pierces** the **empty restraints** of a single **fasting day**.
The **path ahead** removes **perils**,
Avoiding **deep ravines**.

This time, I tell you the **root cause**.
**Meritorious practice** succeeds—
The **Penglai Island** brings **eternal peace**.

All **worldly folk** strive to **do something**.
**Honor** and **wealth** are sought in vain,
**Showing off** one’s abilities **does nothing**.

**Silken robes** and **meat feasts** are fought over in **worldly strife**.
Even if you **secure** a **single rank**,
What **is the point**?

*Wang Zhe* **does not strive**.
A **hempen robe** and **paper robe**—
He **suffers nothing**.

**Following the **flow of fate****, coarse food is his daily fare.
Only in **enduring longevity**,
Does the **true external world** recognize **non-action**.

A **single hempen sack**, a **single drift**.
My **three of us** live in the **Pure Dynasty**.
When **hunger** comes, we **pluck** **jade-like herbs**.
**Controlling** the **stomach**,
We **burn water** in the **fire**—
**Wafting sleeves** brush the **wandering winds**.

The **Azure Crane** leads the way ahead,
Treading the **cloud-tips**.

**Penglai Must Visit Old Wang Qiao.**
We **reaffirm our vow**—
Together we ascend to the **Celestial Dao**.

**Again, a dream:**
I dreamt of a cow before the street.
Its gait was steady, its nature gentle.
When pulled by rope, it turned its head.
On lofty peaks, it trod the moonlit heights—
Most **elegant in its freedom**.
**Follow me** as we wander at will.
In **harmony with the True**, we find **effortless joy**—
No sorrow lingers.
Its **pure white body** is worth lingering with.
**Transcending the mortal shore**, we enter **Yingzhou together**.

**Laughing in bewilderment**, I fail to awaken from illusion.
My **stubborn heart** is locked tight—
How can it open?
Even if wealth and rank bring no calamity,
**Heaven’s allotted span** will claim you in the end.
**Ghostly messengers** hasten your departure.
Sons and grandsons cannot **replace** you—
What **use is delay**?
Only then do you **wail in bitter regret**.
Now you know—
**Cultivating the Dao** is the **true material for transcendence**.

**Again, a Dao-friend inquires:**
**Nurture your nature**—
Do not **let anger arise**.
**Recognize the true body** within,
The **true head** that wraps it.
Daily **practice kindness** as **skillful means**.
**Cool clarity** resides
In **qi and spirit**.
**Avoid wealth and desire**.
**Naturally**, the **Great Dao** opens—
Awakening, **bright and clear**.
When the **Golden Elixir** is perfected,
You **cross the illusory ford**.

「Ascend the Cloud Path, gaze upon the Jade Cavern’s Eternal Spring.
In the Chrysanthemum Realm—
Flesh sells pastries, wine sells oil—
Nourish your body, not your gluttony.
Children and grandchildren frolic in play.
Gold and silver, jewels and treasures,
Piled like mountains and hills.
Why not seek the Dao’s path instead, leaving this transient world behind?
For when your Heavenly allotted span is reached,
Ghostly messengers will come to drag you away.
Only then will you realize your lifetime was all in vain—
Nodding, nodding,
Regretful beyond measure.

I earnestly advise my kin to cease their self-torment,
Knowing each day they dwell in mortal abodes.
Sleeping until the sun is high—
On days when flowers are sold,
There lies a deeper, hidden mystery.
This place, from the start, is truly magnetic—
Naturally quenching flames and dispelling smoke.
To enter the Path of No-Birth,
One must summon the Dao—
Only within the heart’s field.

Again, the spring arrives, yet emptiness remains.
Today’s handful of gentle breeze
Lets me drift like a wandering reed.
Before, I roamed the Cloud-Waters—
The Great Path stretches endlessly.
Though my heart may grow sluggish, my body must not lag,
For I know the finest medicine is *Xion* [芎].
Once taken, my body grows light and strong—
With accumulated virtue and merit,
I must ascend to the vault of Heaven.

**Preface to *Lín Jiāng Xiān*** [临江仙]:
Traveling through the capitals, prefectures, and counties,
And further still to towns, villages, and streets—
No skill or method can bind their endless chatter.
All is truly the same,
As the six senses clamor in iron-like discord.
Do not blame the constant echoes of pure sounds,
Nor those who call you forth from the household gate.
Polish your heart-mirror, lest it grow dim.
A full wheel of moonlight shines clear,
Its light piercing through Kunlun’s heights.
If you govern yourself and practice without faltering,
Your sincere heart will ascend to Heaven’s will.
Within, your essence is refined and radiant.
The numinous and true are sought with clarity—
Only then may you gaze upon the distant.

Hold fast with utmost reverence and single-minded devotion,
In stillness, pure and wrapped in return.
Rely upon the precepts, never straying.
The Nine Mysteries and Seven Ancestors,
Now join you in ascent together.

Master the precepts, guard them with constant care,
Bestow virtue upon all—your merit is foremost.
Your filial heart aligns with the divine.
Enduring and self-perfected,
Forever gazing upon your ancestral ties.
This is the true path of cultivation,
Unbiased and without faction.
Release your heart’s moon to illumine the Golden Lotus.
Fragrant incense ascends to the Azure Han,
Worthy to offer to the Great Luo Daoists.

**Again, on the Four Symbols** [四象]:
The nature of life and death, yin and yang—
If these may be discussed,
Then the heart, spleen, kidneys, and lungs are like a surgeon’s blade.
Further still, the south, north, east, and west.
The celestial stems and branches—
Jia, Geng, Ding, and Gui,
The birds and beasts—Wu, Ju, Hu, and Long.
Child and Midday harmonize, connecting Mao and You.
Spring, winter, autumn, and summer walk hand in hand.
White, green, red, and black—
The rainbow’s hues are revealed.
Kàn, Lí, Zhèn, and Duí—
Water, fire, wood, and metal ascend.

**Again, on the Gourd** [葫芦]:
One gourd, truly excellent—
Each day it follows me.
Its belly is bright, its core is empty.
It stores the elixir of jade and essence,
A taste surpassing even curdled milk.
Drink it daily, and it remains ever full—
No need for coin to buy.
With my staff, I lift it to the Cloud-Way.
Before the Three Pure Ones,
I pass through the Millet, Pearl, and Jade.
The crimson canopy is raised today once more,
And the pomegranate flowers bloom in time.
Who in this gathering understands the harm of the wind?
The Four *Wú* [梧] know my intent,
The Three *Yào* [耀] dispel my misfortune.
Having met, do not grow intoxicated—
Within the cave, there’s another feast.
A single cup avoids the wheel of rebirth.
Naturally, clouds fill my vision—
With each step, I reach Penglai.

**Again, a Dao-friend asks about cultivation:**
Purify yourself, preserve your heart for great goodness,
Ever act with compassion and kindness.
Observe the virtues of mercy and tranquility often.
The profound meanings of the Three Teachings,
All are fully realized here.
Renouncing wife and child is the highest noble,
Abandoning all wealth and desire is the true feast.
Nourish the five viscera to gain longevity.
Merit fulfilled and virtue complete—
With a straightforward nature, you enter the Daoists’ hall.

The *Tàiyī Hùnyuán* [太一混元] true scriptures of the Dao,
With a clear heart and sharp essence, practice with resolve.
First ensnare your own demonic corpse.
The Two *Xiāng* [香] lead to the upper realm,
Their power quietly applied.
Rescue lost souls, dissolve past karmas—
Seeing them preserved, you gain boundless blessings.
Ghosts tremble, spirits are awestruck by the pursuit.
The merit is evident—
Soon, colored clouds will follow you.»

「Drink the golden waves of the Western River’s water,
Each morning using this to swirl and cleanse.
Its cycle flows and turns back to pure spring.
The flesh and skin grow luminous and clear,
Longevity’s measure is prolonged.
The Northern Dipper naturally binds your lineage,
The Southern Star grants a birth for long years.

To reduce wealth and curb desires is the cause and condition—
To take Heaven as your reliance,
Abandon the world to become an Immortal.

Again, **目贻** [Mùyí]—
Why do you love alcohol so madly, like a gust of wind?
It is not because of foolishness, nor do you hold it so lightly.
This Daoist vision sees most clearly.
The Three Paths at the crown become manifest,
You gain companionship with the Daoist’s way.

The Three Teachings’ mysteries are profound and vast,
Yet still you cultivate their wondrous principles.
The Qilin first awakens to Zhongni’s [仲尼] cup,
The Azure Goat speaks to Yinxi’s [尹喜] insight,
The Relic calls to the Attendant Oriole [眷莺].

Again, **题赠道友** [Dìzèng Dàoyǒu]—
[□□] seeks the marvelous methods of Master Du,
[□□] first pursues the Dao’s foundation.
[□□] knows to grasp and modify with urgency.
[□□]’s affection is severed,
[□□] then turns back.
[□□]’s black smoke is all dispelled,
[□□] emerges without a care.
[□□]’s friends are clouds and companions are mists.
On the [□□]’s path to Peng Island,
Together we wander.
[□□]’s consort is now matched as a pair,
[□□] rides the tiger and seizes the dragon.
[□□] sets up a triple-layered pavilion.
[□□]’s spouse is beautiful,
[□□] follows with delight.
Before noon and after childbirth, [□□] refines,
The crimson glow is now complete.
[□□] dwells in the Vermilion Chamber.
On the [□□]’s path beyond the clouds,
[□□] reaches the Peng Palace.
In times of prosperity, [□□] must remain silent,
[□□]’s clarity earns the name *Dèng* [澄].
[□□] utterly abandons, utterly lacks power.
The [□□]’s pavilion enjoys fine scenery,
[□□] ascends in reliance.

The tea of Zhaozhou is of matchless quality,
[□□]’s enlightenment is as clear as water.
Cloud-friends and mist-companions,
[□□]’s parting is achieved,
[□□]’s ascent is now unceasing.

**Dìng Fēng Bō** [定风波]:
Each day, leisurely roaming west and east,
Living in dust, yet passing with the tide of fate.
Faint and boundless—ancient and modern alike—
Enshrouded in harm, like a drifting reed in the wind.
You only know of ants’ fleeting stirrings,
I now love the full bloom of the red hall.
The *Zhāoyī* [昭一] dispels the darkness of former years,
Empty and void, my spirit-refinery pierces the vaulted heavens.

Once, the first stage at Mount Jia,
Now, the Minister’s Sea bears its pure waters.
Again I cross the Jade Pool, truly attaining,
Abundant and bright, my head held high—
My own voice now recognized.
Moonlit silver waves and distinct scenery,
Jade tides and crimson currents earn high renown.
A white lotus rises, one bloom,
Fragrant and clear, it ascends straight into the Great Luo [罗] City.

**Tì Yín Dēng** [剔银灯]:
Now, I renew my awakening with deep sincerity.»

The primordial essence, unchanging from the beginning—
Swiftly cultivate with utmost sincerity,
Full and perfect, meticulously refined to its true form.
Transmit the Mysterious and Pass it on.
Through refining and tempering, it emerges—
Naturally serene and pure.
A single luminous pearl, worthy of reverence,
Now polished to radiant clarity.
Without the Original Master’s guidance,
The Three True Ones would not have arrived,
Nor would the Void-Space Sages gather to rejoice.
This celestial maiden’s fate was preordained here.
**Fēng Mǎ Lìng** [风马令]:
Tame the wind-horse—do not let it run wild.
On the long embankment, the *lúdīng* [瑠玎] drips clear.
At the trough’s head, the monkey plays its tricks.
Hooves gathered, ears pricked—it stands poised in the wind,
The *lúdīng* drips.
The tether on the stake is tightly bound to its shoe.
This time, you—*lúdīng* gleams.
When fully tamed, lead it back to the White Cloud Cave.
Even then, it won’t stay—*lúdīng* shines.

**Bǔ Suàn Zǐ** [卜算子·带暍马]:
First glimpsed, the green steel blade,
Within the corpse, its mark was set.
Planted on wood, a single thread emerged—
The *Gān Mǎ* [乾马] foretold,
After harm, the Wind Platform’s fate.
With this practice, progress grows daily,
Again and again, gathered.
In secret joy, only I know—
The Celestial Horse gazes,
Proving my eternal life.

**Yòu #2 Yè Yǒu Bù Yù** [又#2谒友不遇]:
Once, I saw Master Zhang,
Asking him to inscribe my heart’s intent.
King Rǎn [王喆] comes today, lingering near,
Yet no one stands close enough.
Turning back, I ride the clear breeze,
Clouds and mist follow my steps.
Returning to the Full Truth’s old hall,
I reclaim my luminous clarity.

**Tè Dì Xīn** [特地新]:
Heaven, Earth, and human life—
All gathered here to meet.
What must be made manifest and clear?
The Dao’s gate opens,
The Release’s gate unfolds,
The Confucian path is walkable.
Know the Primordial Origin,
Practice the Primordial Root,
Observe the Primordial Moment—
The Primordial Yang solidifies itself.
Sun, moon, stars—
All revolve in their courses.
Only when the Void is illuminated,
Do the *jīng* gates seal,
The *qi* gates open,
The *shén* gates transcend and reveal.
Drawing from the Three Powers,
Establishing the Three Teachings,
Attaining the Three Lights—
The Three Elixir Treasures converge.

**Quàn Shì** [劝世]:
Showing off skills and feats,
The body displays its forms.

「脱去衣衫，频频更换。 走遍茶坊酒店，总爱夸耀英雄。 忽见天高云淡，这豪情，早已减半。 再劝诸君，莫要迷恋红尘。 保护元阳，切莫让它白白耗散。 轻轻回头，睁开道眼，观看金莲。 玉花绽放，奇香飘来，吐出光明，满空辉煌。

**上林春令** [Shàng Lín Chūn Lìng]:
云水王三悟三悟，甘河镇祖师遇遇。 元本灵明便惺惺，也真个，诗词做做。
丹药内中频顾顾，逍遥处三光觑觑。 全得当时害风风，□真个神仙去去。
晴空如青玉案，放开心月，慧灯明照，两曜交光灿烂。 球装七宝玲珑焕，把性烛当中按。 一对金童呈手段。
琼杵推转，顺风归去，衮入那蓬莱观。

**带马行** [Dài Mǎ Xíng]:
亘初独许能骑坐，这骏驷，从牵拖。 直走盘旋双庆贺。
三山骨健，力筋偏大，马辅佐，万丈红崖过。 谢伊驰出深坑祸，衒玉辔，金缨亸。
喧嘶风雨游水火。 月华前面，四蹄轻锁，马负荷，与我成因果。
元初一得从初遇，便端正昭彰着。 转作重阳晨彩煦。
晴空来往，碧霄堪住，琼马腑，引入长生步。 灵光不动神光聚，便攒簇银霞护。
满插金花频返顾。 青衣鸾鹤，共同来赴，瑶马驻，般在清凉路。

**缘化子弟** [Yuán Huà Zǐdì]:
□□锁户真成也，□□百朝，甚惺惺洒。
□□冰餐非苟且。 □□玄妙，就中超亸，□□马，□□眸粘惹。
□□恩爱俱齐舍，□□□，闲游冷。 □□教余同幽雅。
□□仙子，共成修写，□□马，□□明星下。

**瑞鹧鸪** [Ruì Zhègū]:
昨朝今日与来朝，饮水无加只自浇。 醉后怨铺金藓甲，醒时复采玉芝苗。
锦衣公子谈三岛，皂帔佳人舞六么。 一曲合成玄妙处，白云片片恣飘飖。
我咱别有赤穷穷，物物俱无事事通。 清裹清来全寂阒，闲中闲至住虚空。
能邀迥照堪亲日，会捉轻飙便害风。 此际黑云何处去，莹然衮出一团红。
三才剖判做辉华，三教分明吐甲芽。 三宝炼烧红焰宝，三车搬运紫河车。
三峰影裹观真宅，三耀光中是本家。 三岛十洲堪捣药，三清十极聚青霞。
今朝细细问朱郎，因甚常眠黑鬼房？ 得与青龙为伴侣，亦令白虎助清凉。
便将铅汞堪成宝，好把刀圭更入钢。 斫断乌龟四只脚，爽邀风月上昆岗。
堪当姹女嫁丁郎，认得婴儿住癸房。 幸有甲田知出入，不无兑地做炎凉。
铅刀起处通神妙，汞剑开时仗慧钢。 杀却三尸阴鬼尽，一团红焰覆琼岗。
白灵根蒂长晴空，碧绿枝条袅细风。 叶禀月华添雅翠，花凭日气蘸殷红。
四般颜色虽然异，一道馨香分外浓。 透过丹霄归甚处，便教收在蕊珠宫。
石中火隐怎生昭，水裹金藏要却遭。 石火须凭心火取，水金决得肺金淘。
火教煅炼真铅汞，金要增添快剑刀。 二件相投成一件，大罗天上列仙曹。
这回捉住四时春，夺得温和养本真。 跳出世情居异世，尽教人道不凡人。
何须苦苦调精气，不在区区嗽液津。 莹处晴空开日月，锐然特放九光新。

**踏莎行** [Tà Shā Xíng]:
东海汪洋，西山详审，金钩钓得欢无恁。 一头活乐大鲸鱼，万鳞灿烂铺白锦。
随我遨游，水云信任，青山绿水相过甚。 张公吃酒李公来，李公夺了张公饮。

**干友打斧** [Gān Yǒu Dǎ Fǔ]:
（The second half of the *带马行* stanza remains untranslated due to missing characters, but the structure continues as follows:）
骏马驰骋，斧劈如风，友情干劲显无穷。

版斧如求，那由选拣，良工欲造无钱换。
The sought-after axe—who dares to choose it? A master craftsman longs to forge it, yet lacks the coin to trade.

今朝专礼我华宗，慈悲为首诸公辨。
Today, I pay homage to our Daoist lineage, where compassion stands foremost—distinguished by all revered masters.

若得坚钢，劈开道眼，灵台熠耀持金简。
Should I obtain unyielding steel, I shall cleave the Dao’s sacred eye—
the luminous spirit platform blazing with golden tablets.

腰间柯烂决忘归，白云路上成家产。
With axe-handle rotting at my waist, I forget all return—
my fortune lies in the paths where white clouds drift.

---
**咏镢**
铁镢神灵，我心有则，随身应手开端的。
The iron hoe’s divine might—my heart holds its essence,
ever at hand, ready to act at the first opportunity.

种成大药称伊功，栽生善果凭君力。
Cultivated into elixir, its merit is his alone;
planted as virtue, its fruit depends on your strength.

锉倒恩山，打摧爱狱，是非烦恼频频雕。
It grinds down the Mountain of Grace, shatters the Prison of Affection—
carving away the ceaseless carvings of strife and vexation.

锐然敲碎赋玞顽，便令发出昆仑玉。
Sharp strikes shatter the stubborn *fuyu*—
and lo, Kunlun jade emerges radiant.

---
**总咏**
斧锲堪擎，随缘斫冲，钢全生就令分局。
The axe and chisel may be wielded—
cutting as fate dictates, steel whole and ready to divide realms.

一司管刮水中金，一司管伐山头玉。
One office scrapes gold from the water’s depths,
another fells jade from the mountain’s peak.

窍子方长，攀儿圆促，头头柄柄常相逐。
The holes are long and square, the claws round and tight—
each head and handle ever in pursuit.

劈开金母紫芒攒，判通玉祖红光簇。
It splits the Golden Mother’s violet rays,
and cleaves the Jade Ancestor’s crimson luminosity.

---
**咏宦途无定**
名路求高，宦途无定，一来一去缘心性。
The path to renown is ever shifting—
officialdom’s way is uncertain, coming and going as one’s nature dictates.

稍知分守得优游，能通止足参贤圣。
A modest understanding of duty brings ease;
to master restraint is to consort with sages.

莫使偏颇，须存直正，花开须是依时令。
Do not stray from rectitude—
uprightness must be preserved, like flowers blooming in season.

日轮耀处吐光辉，月华朗后添清莹。
Where the sun’s wheel shines, radiance is cast forth,
and moonlight brightens with added clarity.

---
**渔父咏（渔家傲）**
北海馄鲸人不识，金风长是传消息。
The Northern Sea’s leviathan remains unseen by man—
the golden winds alone bear its tidings.

予把钓车宁费力。
I cast my fishing cart—what labor is this?

堪怜忆，香钩掷下离滩侧。
Pity the memory—
the fragrant hook cast aside where the shallows end.

吐出神珠光焰赫，化鹏展起垂云翼。
It spews forth divine pearls in blazing light,
transforming into a *peng* bird, wings trailing clouds.

日在扶摇无有极。
The sun ascends the *fuyao*—boundless in its rise.

能搏陆，青霄一举应端直。
It can strike the earth—
with one leap to the azure heights, upright and true.

---
**咏假俏汉**
奸点人人常不逊，外装内喜能谈论。
The deceitful mark is ever insolent—
externally adorned, inwardly delighted in idle chatter.

艳色衣裳香远喷。
His garish robes reek of perfume from afar.

频整顿，重重结裹粗如囤。
Frequently adjusted, layer upon layer,
bundled coarsely like a granary’s store.

眼去眉来常骋俊，前攀后拽夸身分。
His eyes and brows ever display cunning—
climbing forward, dragging behind, boasting of his station.

我便去前·亲去问。
I step forward to inquire directly.

休风韵，遮藏臭腐并堆粪。
Avoid his hollow elegance—
he conceals rot and piles dung.

---
**闲题**
生死轮回何太速，改颜换面人难识。
The wheel of life and death turns too swiftly—
faces change, and few recognize the shift.

有个风狂常自足。
There is one mad with wind, ever self-satisfied.

常自足，逍遥处处孤眠宿。
Ever self-sufficient, he drifts alone,
sleeping wherever the wind takes him.

愁煞诸公欢折哭，恰如堂下三间屋。
He vexes all with his joyous weeping—
like three rooms beneath a hall.

屋底你咱烦恼黑。
Within those rooms, our vexations fester dark.

烦恼黑，堂中我且燃灯烛。
Vexation’s darkness—
while I light lamps in the hall above.

---
**赠友人**
□□名宦为盐判，□□室内同公案。
[Name] holds office as a salt magistrate,
[Name]’s chamber shares the same official bench.

「□□ with idle thoughts, each half their own.
□□ praises, □□ divides—how can one sever?
□□ loves to keep company with clouds and waters,
□□ watches husband and wife atop the mountains.

□□ calls with the clear wind and bright moon.

□□ plays, □□ binds—
a boundless tally of entanglements.

The **River Transmission** decree: *"Bamboo crowns pressed to the top,*
*more bamboo as water bottles—*
*to this day, they still wash their hands with them."*

Bamboo staff, bamboo basket,
bamboo hat, bamboo cart, bamboo bundles.
In the bamboo grove,
the bamboo flute sighs,
its voice calling itself.

Wooden sandals pad the feet with true warmth,
wooden bowls polished—
mirrors round and flawless.

Wooden chopsticks, wooden spoons,
wooden ladles, wooden helmets, wooden bowls.
In the wooden shade,
the wooden ox plows,
three fields in a row.

With skillful means to sustain the body,
this hunger and cold are not escaped—
on the street, one must still beg for alms.

Lifting a pure and clear vessel,
bright and lucid as iron—
*□□* (awakened awareness).

Seeking what remains,
calling out, call after call,
**Dao/Way** seizes the chaos.

At the **Noble Residence**’s mercy, sighs resound—
I only hope that all may,
with hearts ever compassionate, take care.

Choose what’s cold to eat,
later to be seared in the belly’s crucible.
Refining the **Heavy Yang** (elixir),
one may then behold—
the **Dao/Way**-harmed man.

**Dao/Way**-harmed, fallen and broken,
he drifts like a tumbleweed in trust,
nowhere to rest, no fence to lean.

Roaming waters and clouds,
what matters if the body decays?
Seeking what remains,
near others’ homes,
in empty courtyards.

All laugh at my poverty and decline—
let them see my bones,
unfated to linger long.

Look how you don’t know—
where will you end up?

Avoid his sorrow—
when that time comes,
ascend to the **Blue Detached** (pure realm).

Ordinary flesh, no reliance—
take this lucid, awakened awareness,
and naturally the structure will be clear.

In walking, standing, sitting, or lying,
one must ever be serene and unburdened.

**Qi** and spirit harmonized,
form a pearl—
worthy of transformation.

Drawing bow and shooting arrow, he can strike true,
his **virtue/power** (red heart) piercing,
driving back the **Zhou Tian** (cosmic cycles).

Within the **stacked layers** (of the body),
entering and exiting—
priceless radiance like mist.

The **Five Phases** (elements) transgressed,
escaping **Yin-Yang**,
surpassing **Creation** (natural order).

Lamenting the **fragrant moment**—
by **heavy fate**, hands bound, feet planted.

---
*(Note: Some characters remain unclear or ambiguous—□□, "□□", "周天卦", "垛贴", "五行违", "造化", "重阳", "害风汉", "碧落", "惺惺", "了了", "周天卦", "周天", "周天" are left untranslated where context is insufficient. "周天" may refer to Daoist cosmological cycles, while "害风汉" likely denotes a Daoist adept or practitioner suffering from external influences.)*

「Suddenly attaining the true and true without error.
A golden furnace stands, a jade flower blooms.
Refined by fire, this elixir emerges—
Three Fields and Nine Circulations radiant with dazzling light.
The Eight Vessels ascend, opening the Four Gates—
Voidness itself becomes a single, scorching point.
Wordless, yet naturally inviting.

All who study the Dao should be few.
Carefully grasp the subtle mysteries, ever unfolding.
At the head’s edge, recognize the Cooling Pillow.
When wind and moon meet, luminous repose is achieved.

The taste of the Swords of Immortality is savored again and again.
Gradually, a thousand petals bloom like embroidered silk.
Fragrance as profound as the Dao’s essence—
Lamenting the fragrant moment, savoring its hidden worth.

---
**Ode to the Purple Swallow**
I observe the purple swallow building its mud nest.
Daily it hatches eggs, cradling its young.
The fledglings grow, leaving the nest to rise—
Abandoning their parents, flying away.
For mortals, nurturing the small is like this:
Though they know how to climb, the bonds grow ever hotter.
Better to cultivate the Way of Eternal Life,
To delight in pure leisure, wandering among clouds and waters.

---
**On a Friend’s Inquiry About Yin-Yang**
Before Yin and Yang were divided, where was there form?
Only when Heaven’s height and Earth’s depth were settled.
Then Buqian and Kun separated, the Three Lights shone.
Within the body, the **Yin-Yang** (□□) **harmony** (冲和) **runs wild** (奔走).
Fire arises in water, battling again and again.
Then the White Tiger and Green Dragon engage in union.
Male and female offspring guard one another.
But the **Daoist adept** (害风汉) has other companions.

---
**Purple Swallow Returns** (青玉案带马行)
A blessed omen grows from the **Fuxiang Tree** (扶桑), a rare herb.
Planted then in **Penglai Island** (蓬莱),
Its golden branches and jade leaves are naturally fine,
On **Kunlun Mountain** (昆仑), they transform into treasures.
Mist radiates in all directions, deepening the mystery,
Flames envelop, dispelling confusion.
The **Celestial Attendants** (青童) present decrees, adding auspicious titles—
In the realm of **Wuwei** (无为), this is its return.

---
**The Spring Festival Command** (青玉案)
The true nature is vast and silent,
Hidden yet boundless, neither minute nor grand.
A cluster of luminous gems,
Bright light encircling, five colors in harmony.
Effortlessly wandering, worthy of passage—
With a **Jade Boy** (玉童) in attendance.
Filling the void with fragrance and richness,
Overflowing, it enfolds the face—
To accompany the **Immortal Ones** (神仙) in their gathering.

---
**A Hundred Years’ Reflection in the Mirror** (南乡子)
A hundred years’ visage in the mirror’s gaze,
Raising hands to bless, yet hands turn cruel.
Life and death, honor and decay—all now before my eyes.
Do not meet (this fate).
Swiftly return to the heart, recognize the **Ancestral Dao** (祖宗).
The **perfect forms** (得得妙相) follow,
Extinguishing the **Three Corpses and Nine Parasites** (三尸九虫).
**Qi** (一气) vast and serene, nurtured aright,
Purified—
The **Blue Rabbit** (兔击) **refines** (精蓝) beyond mortal measure.

---
**End of Volume Twelve of the *Zhongyang Quanzhen Collection*** (重阳全真集卷之十二竟)

---
**End of Volume Thirteen of the *Zhongyang Quanzhen Collection*** (重阳全真集卷之十三终) */by **Master Zhongyang of Chongnan Mountain, Wang Zhe** (终南山重阳子王哲撰).*

---
**Lyric Title: *望蓬莱* (望江南)**»**

**A Hundred Years’ Reflection in the Mirror** (南乡子)

---

**#1 On Parting from a Daoist Friend**
Wang Zhe has already migrated eastward,
Passing the assembly of sages at Ganhé River.
Internal hunger and cold still plague my being,
Travel expenses—beg from the virtuous among you, let them grant their own coins.
**Perfect forms** (得得) pass one to another,
Enlightening us both as we emerge from the Nine-Lotus [1].
How many hearts now grasp this truth?
Pitying, pitying—this parting carries the **Buddha’s original qi** (本气) onward.

I have now arrived in Nanjing,
Where every person in Gānzhèn knows my name.
Respect the **Three Lights** (三光) and recognize their essence,
Do not slight the **Five Grains** (五谷) within which the **vital essence** (精) is refined.
This journey marks my final course,
And I have set down my life’s own voice in writing.
If we meet again in this world,
Souls vividly—we shall behold the **true form**, **one qi** (一气) pure and clear.

Wealth and poverty alike may visit the body,
Yet one must embrace honor and decay with **virtue** (仁) alone.
Preordained fate now finds its use in this life,
With a pure heart—
**Ancestral merit** (阴功) and **blessings** (福) naturally attain perfection.

Do not further endure hardship’s bitterness,
Nor cling to wrongdoing—seek **auspicious causes** (善因) instead.
I urge the bewildered to awaken and reflect,
Do not harbor resentment—
All things follow **Heaven’s will** (天), not man’s.

---

**#2 *Wu Ling Spring* (武陵春)**
Charge the **Duke of Yan** (阎公) to return to his ancestral home,
And convey my words to the **Lingquan people** (醴泉人).
Do not lament their **greed** (贪求) or **anger** (嗔),
For they gain **vital spirit** (好精神).
This alone suffices as the **Great Dao** (大道),
Why seek **ultimate truth** (真) in vain?
If all can awaken to this **body** (此身),
Then they may emerge from the **dust of the world** (嚣尘).

---

**#3 *Bai Fei Lang* (买费笼)**
Willow branches supple, hemp threads fine,
A **mysterious hand** (妙手) binds with **arcane skill** (玄功).
**Subtle recognition** (密识) secures the **tightly knotted constraints** (牢缠系),
Fashioning the **body** (身儿) to perfection.

---

**#4 *On the Feast of Lingquan* (咏馎托)**
The inn is fine,
The **lingquan feast** (馎托) most wondrous and rare.
Endless **jade flakes** (玉屑) kneaded into dough,
A single **pearl-like flour sheet** (琼瑶) spread smooth and even,
Now let the **treasured blade** (宝刀) cut it clean.

To the **masterful hand** (妙手),
With steady intent—arrange it well.
Like **plum blossoms** (梨花) fresh upon a dish,
Silken strands of **silver threads** (银线) delicately lifted,
Feast upon it and hasten to **Penglai** (蓬莱).

---

**#5 *On Exhorting a Daoist Fellow* (咏劝道友)**
Duke Zhao is fine,
His noble bearing radiant in the prime of **Spring** (青春).
Do not let **light and time** (光阴) slip away in vain,
But earnestly cultivate **meritorious deeds** (功行) to draw near the **true essence** (实相).
Let us dwell as neighbors in the **Dao**.

**Serene and free** (清闲),
One must know the **crossing of delusion** (迷津).
A moment’s awakening dispels the **floating life** (浮生) of clinging desires,
As one understands the **illusionary nature** (幻化) and abandons **greed and wrath** (贪嗔),
Then is he a **hermit of the cave** (洞中人).

Not yet in the **Dao** (未入道),
Do not cling to **half-truths** (中迷).
First, **seize firmly** (牢擒) the **lowly horse** (劣马子),
And **bind tightly** (缚住) the **playful monkey** (耍猿儿).
Step by step, **cultivate with patience** (修持).

If one **awakens** (省悟),
Then **discern** (勘破) the **husband-wife bonds** (女男妻).
**At ease in the假 body**, ever **refining** (煅炼),
The **true nature** (真性) drifts freely—**pushed along** (推移),
Surely one attains the **Upper Pool of Reeds** (瑶池).

My words are earnestly offered,
Now is the time to **cultivate well** (持修).
**Fleeting fame and profit** (浮名浮利) when shall they end?
**Exhausting spirit and qi** (劳神劳气) when shall they rest?
Do not linger in the **dusty world** (尘世).

Awaken soon,
The **three teachings** (三教) hold **profound mysteries** (理玄幽).
Shake off the **Mountain of Karma** (恩山) and dispel the **Sea of Attachment** (爱海),
Return to **Penglai Island** (蓬岛) and journey to **Yingzhou** (瀛洲),
For all is **here, within this heart** (在此心头).

My words awaken understanding,
Now is the time to **cultivate well** (修修).
**Monkey-mind** (意马) and **wandering thoughts** (心猿) must all be **seized**,
Clinging affections and desires—**all must cease**,
Do not delay in **auspicious deeds** (善事).

The **three teachings** (三教) are fine,
Their **wondrous principles** (妙理) most profound and subtle.
Cast off the **floating life** (浮生) and **worldly affairs** (世事),
This time, the path ahead leads to **Penglai** (蓬洲),
Here lies the **true return** (归头).

---

**#6 *On the Apricot Blossom* (题杏花)**
Spring’s scene is fine,
Apricot blooms blush with crimson cheeks.
Laughing at the sun, its **divine form** (仙姿) truly beautiful,
Leaning into the wind, its tender face most wondrous and rare—
Not even the **plum of winter** (腊前梅) can compare.

Who truly knows?
Only the blossoms **allow me** (许) to gaze upon them.
I pluck a single branch to hold in hand,
Its fragrance fills my sleeves—let it return as it will,
I shall take you to **Penglai** (蓬莱).

---
**End of Volume Thirteen of the *Zhongyang Quanzhen Collection*** (重阳全真集卷之十三终) */by **Master Zhongyang of Chongnan Mountain, Wang Zhe** (终南山重阳子王哲撰).*

---

**#6 *On the Apricot Blossom* (题杏花)**
Worthy to compare with the **Ode of King Wen** (王风),
A family’s fortune grows on its back.
**Roaming in the water-clouds** (水云游), its **spiritual nature** (灵性) and **wisdom** (慧) refined—
Its **use of food and clothing** (衣餐) and **deep-rooted face** (裹面) reveal its **true essence** (深根蒂).
To strip away the **coarse mortal body** (凡躯) and solve the riddle—
**Clarity dawns** (了了), **transcending** (超升) to its **divine form** (伊相).
*(End of Volume Thirteen of the *Zhongyang Quanzhen Collection*)*

---

**#7 *Instructing a Daoist Friend** (点化道友)**
Each and every one,
Ever guards their ** Daoist path** (铺).
The **Elder wraps them** (翁裹) beneath a **single hood** (合头),
Bound by **iron cords** (铁索) in **mystic ties** (缠缚).
How can they know its **radiant origin** (光耀处)?
It is **Divine Immortals** (神仙)—why not **open their hearts** (开心) and **awaken** (悟)?
Seek the **cool refuge** (清凉),
Gather **steady steps** (稳步).
If they wish to **drift to Penglai** (飘蓬),
Only **mad winds** (狂风) will suffice.
Or they may **lean upon clouds and waters** (依凭云水).
To claim **serene leisure** (清闲),
And walk the **Path of Effortless Wandering** (逍遥路).

Each and every one,
**Two months and eight days** (二旬八).
Do not **turn back** (回头),
Or their **life and vitality** (性命) will be **scoured away** (搜刷).
They’ll fall into **endless ruin** (沉沦),
Crushed beneath **constant pressure** (坠压).
When the **mirror** (镜子) is brought near,
What **words** (言) can they **answer** (谈答)?
It is **Divine Immortals** (神仙)—why not **perceive** (察)?
**Sever the mortal heart** (劈破凡心),
And **recognize the Buddha and Bodhisattvas** (佛菩萨).
A **single luminous pearl** (明珠) is polished again and again—
In the **Seven Treasures Palace** (七宝宫),
A **true golden tower** (真金塔) is raised.

---

**#8 *Giving to a Daoist Friend** (赠同友)**
This **Flower Sect** (华宗),
Can **follow my Way** (顺我).
With **pure intentions** (净意) and **clear heart** (清心),
They **recognize the Effortless Rest** (逍遥卧).
Daily, they **hide from the mundane** (便躲).
They **take the Daoist Master** (教公) as their own,
Finding **joy unbroken** (快乐).

**Turn back early** (早回头),
Do not **drift past** (休漫过).
**Extinguish all ignorance** (灭尽无明),
And **distance the ordinary passions** (远了寻常火).
A **single spark of Dao** (灵光) is locked upon the mountain.
**Steady their ride** (稳驾) on the **White Clouds** (白云),
And **sit within the Five-Colored Mists** (五色霞).

---

**#9 *Lamenting a Friend’s Body** (咏友人叹身)**
Reflect upon their **form** (身),
Seal their **mouth** (口).
They’ve **won serene leisure** (赢得清闲),
And **roam in effortless ease** (逍遥走).
As **fate allows** (随分),
They **should live forever** (应永久).
**Unrighteous wealth** (不义之财),
Let them **shrink back** (且缩) and **hold fast to the Clouds** (拏云手).

**Little by little** (少追陪),
**Sip wine lightly** (微饮酒).
**Moderate their desires** (节色),
And **search their original purity** (搜身).
They **recognize the Three Lights** (三光) and **filial piety** (兼孝),
And **friendly virtue** (友).
They **do not pray to deities** (不祝神祇),
Yet still **gain eternal spring** (也得长春寿).

---

**#10 *White Admonition to a Daoist Friend** (白告友人)**
In the **prime of youth** (正青春),
Their **ruddy faces** (红貌) gather.
**Bitterly** (苦肯) they **turn back** (回头),
Now **clearly** (分明) they **glimpse** (觑).
I wish they’d **awaken early** (心早悟).
**Live as neighbors to the Dao** (与道为邻),
And **dwell in effortless ease** (也处逍遥所).

**Good fate comes** (善缘来),
**Bad fate departs** (恶缘去).
They **see the true form** (搜见真容),
And **know it resides in the Spirit Platform** (灵台住).
The **Seven Seats** (七座) open,
Connecting to the **Great Ancestor** (的祖).
When they **leap free** (跳出),
They **enter the Path of Eternal Life** (便入长生路).

---

**#11 *Giving to a Daoist Friend** (赠于道友)**
To **practice the Dao** (修行),
They must **strive with resolve** (须发愤).
**Abandon all worries** (除了忧愁),
And **cut through all emotional vexations** (破尽情怀闷).
**Wield the Wisdom Blade** (□仗慧刀) to **sever the Five Aggregates** (挥五蕴).
**Split the dual gates** (劈开双关),
And **steadily attain the Three Divisions** (稳稳成三分).

**No bargaining** (没商量),
**No questioning** (休厮问).
Only **repeatedly recite the previous verses** (搬运前篇),
Daily, **polishing them** (日日频).

**Good to seek in their own homes** (好向家中搜),
**Dung and ordure** (土粪).
**Uncover the luminous pearl** (拨见明珠),
And **carry it to the Cool Refuge Domain** (携入清凉郡).

---

**#12 *Giving to a Daoist Friend** (赠于道友)
To **cultivate the Classics well** (善修文),
They **can pass the imperial examinations** (能应举).
Why not **seek the Nine-Turn Elixir** (九转金丹)?
If they **turn back and glance** (若肯回头时暂觑),
Their **feet grow light and reckless** (两足轻狂),
And they **step into the Cloud-and-Mist Path** (走入云霞步).
**Align with the Three Lights** (按三光),
**Follow the Master** (随师父).
There is **another Path** (别有一条),
**Steadily leading to Eternal Life** (稳稳长生路).
**Freely wandering**, they **open the Jade Gate** (自在逍遥开玉户).
**Good to join the Royal Wind** (好与王风),
**Together returning on the appointed day** (指日同归去).

---

**#13 *Instructing the Disciples** (训徒众)
Brothers **burdened with doubt** (弟兄懑),
**Struggle to act** (争下手).
**Clashing with the world** (与世相违),
They **must daily restrain their speech** (日日长钤口).
**Do not speak of mercury, lead, or the hours of Mao and You** (休论汞铅并卯酉).
**Open and expound the Vermilion Palace** (开阐绛宫),
And **freely wander** (自在逍遥走).
The **Two Principles are true** (二仪真),
The **Three Radiances are refined** (三耀秀).
Though I **wish to transmit in person** (我欲亲传),
I **do not yet grant fulfillment** (未肯相成就).
Only when they **observe the currents together** (直待同流观得透),
**Calmly halting their ascent** (款款停腾),
**Dare they reveal the Heavenly Mechanism** (敢把天机漏)?
**Ask the True Cultivator** (问真修),
**Listen to my judgment** (听我断).
**Do not cling to the mortal form** (莫着凡躯),
**Frequently pondering all things** (物物频思算).
**Shatter all conventional notions** (打破般般常内看).
In **sitting, lying, walking, or dwelling** (坐卧行住),
They **must observe as a skeleton** (须作骷髅观).
**Gradually perfecting this** (渐令成),
They **must diligently align** (常谨按).
The **Eight-Mu Jade Field** (八亩琼田)
Holds **another refined method** (别有新条段).
**Nature’s clarity is plain for proper contemplation** (性上分明堪正玩).
**Measuring without error** (量得无差),
They **reach the Cool Refuge Shore** (便到清凉岸).

**The Dao is wordless** (道无言),
**Zen is unsaid** (禅没说).
Two **rays of white light** (两道白光),
Only **allowing the Red Mist to set** (唯许红霞设).
On **True Jade Mountain**, they **constantly pull and tug** (真玉山头常摆拽).
**Splendid and bright** (泼滟滟兮),
**Reflecting upon the Spirit Peak’s snow** (返照灵峰雪).
**Ever more refined** (愈玲珑),
**Yet more luminous** (尤皎洁).
**Piercing the clear sky** (射透晴空),
**Distinct divine light** (莹莹神光别).
At this **profoundly profound mystery** (到此玄玄玄妙彻),
A **golden flower blooms** (一朵金花),
**Enclosing the Elixir’s formation** (裹面金丹结).

---

**#14 *To [Name Redacted] Public** (□邢公, □分剖)
[Name] **holds gratitude** (□举恩情),
**Severing the Spirit Light’s radiance** (割断灵光照).
[Name] **seeks the True Lotus within** (□内莲生真可要).
[Name] **cherishes youthful grace** (□姹婴娇),
**Harmonizing with the profound mystery** (和会通玄妙).
[Name] **abandons sorrow** (□忧愁),
[Name] **finds joy in the Dao** (□乐道).
[Name] **gathers the qi** (□气收来),
**Forming it into a precious treasure** (结作成珍宝).
[Name] **hides the Five-Colored Radiance in the Jade Prison** (□玉牢藏五彩耀).
[Name] **penetrates Kunlun** (□透昆仑),
**Crafting the True Cultivation of Sun and Moon** (日月真修造).

---
**#15 *Washing the Brook Sand** (浣溪沙)
The **Great Dao is nameless yet seems named** (大道无名似有名),
**Bodhidharma faced the wall for nine years in purity** (达磨面壁九年清).
**The Sakyamuni sat in snow for six years in precision** (释迦坐雪六年精).
**Seizing the True Void’s wondrous function** (夺得真空真妙用),
**A single gate enfolds the Round and Bright** (一通门裹出圆明).
**The Great Luo Heaven gathers it into perfection** (大罗天上聚圆成).
**Behold the Void’s Seven-Treasure Garden** (会看虚空七宝园),
**Able to open the Six-Qi Tranquil Pavilion** (能开寂静六华轩).
**Hsi-yi’s subtlety lies in Kun and Qian** (希夷微妙在坤乾).
**Piercing the *Yin Symbol’s* Three Hundred Characters** (理透阴符三百字),
**Searching through the *Dao De Jing’s* Five Thousand Words** (搜通道德五千言).
**Let the Harmful Wind blow as it will** (害风一任害风虔).
Beside **green waters**, they **ascend the Snow Mountain** (绿水傍边上雪山),
**Sharp and leaping**, they **burst from the Jade Gate Pass** (锐然跳出玉门关).
**Void within, empty without**, they **open their faces** (虚中空外一开颜).
**Distant and boundless**, they **return to the True Path** (渺邈那边归正路),
**The very end is the stable dwelling** (的端便是稳居间).

---

**The Pure White Cloud** (White Cloud Difficult to Compare with This Pure Pass)
This **Clear Pass** (清关) surpasses white clouds in purity.

**Again, on the Double Ninth Festival** (重九日)
When the **Golden Tiger** (金虎) roars and the **Golden Horse** (金马) passes,
The **Golden Sage** (金公) scatters **golden coins** (金钱) on the Double Ninth.
Where the **Golden Wind** (金风) blows, **golden ornaments** (金钿) dance.
The **Golden Earth** (金地) spreads with **golden blossoms** (金蕊泛),
And the **Golden Boy** (金童) bends to pluck the **golden lotus steps** (金莲).
A **golden plate** (金盘) wraps his face, offered to the **golden sage** (金仙).
One word alone holds twelve **golden meanings** (十二金),
Practice diligently, seeking **Dao/Way** in daily hours and moments.

**Seizing the Monkey and Horse Tightly** (急将猿马紧牢擒)
The **Five Houses** (五户) naturally open, revealing **dharma** (阐尽),
And the **jade flowers** (玉花) cluster around the **deep cave entrance** (洞门深).
Who from old truly knows the **harmony** (知音)?

**Again, on the Pen** (咏笔)
From the start, the **brush’s tip** (毛颖) held deepest **intent** (意).
Do not let **Jiang Yan’s** dreams (江淹梦裹) stir false thoughts.
Where **Ban Chao** cast his pen (班超投处), follow its traces well.

**Leisure and Freedom** (放逸真闲攞雅致)
In true ease, **refining elegance** (攞雅致) comes naturally—
Poetry and words need not be written to **chant lofty** (高吟).
This time, he **plucks gold from the water** (捞出水中金).

**Recalling Wang Sun** (忆王孙)
Four nights of **delightful reunion** (得得并无寒),
Deep gratitude to **Master Sun** (孙公) for his **favorable glance** (青顾看),
As **crimson sleeves** (霞袖) part, brushing away the **misty ends** (雾端).
Entering **Chang’an** (长安), looking back,
He **teaches the wise** (教贤) to forge the **Great Elixir** (结大丹).
Why return to **Chang’an** (长安)?
It lets my **five-petaled lotus** (莲花五叶) bloom,
With **clear light** (清光) that **once steadied the wine-vat** (旧镇醅).
Alone, I **raise my cup** (倾杯),
Avoiding the **Nine Hells of rebirth** (轮回九狱灾).

**Again, Giving to Ma Yu** (赠马钰)
They say the **mouth is the gate of calamity** (口是祸之门),
But I say the **tongue is the root of calamity** (舌为祸本根).
Silence without speech means no **discussion** (讨论).
Past the **morning and evening darkness** (度朝昏),
One finds **tranquil ease and life-preservation** (安闲保命存).

**Difficult Partings** (离别难)
Traveling through **watery clouds** (水云) of two **prefectures** (郡),
Do not stir **emptiness** (无寥).
Observe the **clear cycles** (清轮), recognize the **windy gusts** (风飙).
The **jewel-like pearls** (琼瑶) gleam,
And **auspicious *qi*** (嘉气) fills the **crimson heaven** (丹霄).
**Jade flowers** (玉花) exhale **fragrant essence** (吐馥郁),
**Golden lotuses** (金莲) emit **sweet scent** (馨香)—
Which of these two **consumes** (消) the other?

**Following Fate** (随缘从)
Covered in **scarlet clouds** (焘红霞缭绕),
The **emerald mist** (翠雾) does not spare.
**Opportunities come** (得得),
**Days shine bright** (昭昭),
Like the **Penglai Isles** (准蓬莱),
**Faith is steadfast** (定信频招).
In the **void**, **rainbow-colored phoenixes** (彩凤) come and go,
And **golden boys** (金童) bear **purple reishi** (紫芝苗) before them.
Now, he **seeks my face again** (觊吾颜),
Unless he can **renew the strings** (续弦断重调).
I urge you all—
**Each must cultivate** (各各修持),
For **one step into the distant cave** (洞天遥) is all.

**Zhao Jun’s Grievance** (昭君怨)
Early, I was **reported to leave the Fire Palace** (离火院),
And **fled a household of clinging affections** (攀恋).
My gaze rests on **watery clouds** (水云) ahead,
In **harmony** (安然).
Then I **refined the Great Elixir** (结长生煅炼),
Becoming a **close kin of the Immortal** (上仙亲眷).
I **plucked the dark secrets from the emerald pond** (搜出碧潭玄),
And the **moon’s circle was whole** (月团圆).

**Pounding the Elixir** (捣练子)
*Pounding the Elixir* (捣练子),
How **ten times** (十怎生) can it be refined?
In **leisure**, one **comes and goes** (闲来闲去) to practice well.
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
If one **welcomes and responds** (逢迎),
It **can be perfected** (得圆成),
From the start, **one by one** (从头一一) explaining the **path ahead** (前程).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
As a **human**, one **takes a mortal form** (做凡身),
How can the **Four Refined Substances** (四般假合) produce the **True Elixir** (怎生真)?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
**Search the Dao’s mysteries** (搜玄路),
**Exit the Confusion’s ford** (出迷津),
In **stillness**, **nourish *qi* and spirit** (调养气精神).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
**Monkey rides the Horse** (猿骑马),
**Showing off its antics** (逞颠耍),
How can one **seize and abandon** (擒捉怎生舍) it?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
The **wise blade** (慧刀) **opens** (开),
**Equalizing and severing** (齐杀下),
Teaching you to **recognize the source and root** (认得根源也),
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
This **Great Perfection** (圆通) **dwells in the Void** (住虚空),
In **obscure depths** (冥冥杳杳), how can it be **exhausted** (怎生穷)?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
**Divide South from North** (分南北),
**Observe West and East** (看西东),
Once **awakened**, it lies only in **laughter and talk** (笑谈中).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
The **Double Ninth Immortal** (重阳子),
**Complete Dao/Way’s truth** (全真理),
How can one **reverse yin and yang** (颠倒怎生使)?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
Here **one practices**, there **one ceases** (这头行，那头止),
**Balancing above and below** (冲和上下) **clearly** (分明是).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
Using the **surgical knife** (刀圭),
**Cutting through confusion** (剖昏迷),
How can one **harmonize and carry** (合和一处怎生携)?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
**Heads fall**, **red lightning appears** (现红霓),
And **white lotus blooms from green mud** (白莲花朵出青泥).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
**Original nature** (从来性),
**Innate fate** (本来命),
Without **form or substance** (无形无质), how can it **awaken** (怎生惺)?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
**Mercury’s clarity** (汞中明),
**Lead’s luminosity** (铅中莹),
**Crimson light wraps the face** (霞光裹面), revealing **sages and saints** (通贤圣).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
**Gold in water** (水中金),
**Too profound and dark** (忒幽深),
In **mysteries deep and subtle** (玄玄妙妙), how can it be **sought** (怎生寻)?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
From **first attainment** (初得),
To **now** (到如今),
The **west wind** (西风) **again and again sends clear sounds** (时复送清音).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
The **Three Elixirs’ treasures** (三丹宝),
**Difficult to divide and refine** (难分剖),
In **dull obscurity** (昏昏默默), how can they be **preserved** (怎生保)?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.
In the **Void**, long **embrace and hold** (长怀抱).

---

**Loose Garments Wrapped in a New Black Hat** (绯衫裹了新乌帽).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.

**Water and Fire combined** (水兼火),
**Kàn and Lǐ intertwined** (坎和离),
How can one **grasp their interplay** (两般消息怎生知)?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.

**Cease not to refine** (休烧炼),
**Do not seek to cultivate** (莫修持),
For **they are but these very things** (元来只是这些儿).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.

On **the Day of Opened Heart** (开心日),
When **perfect clarity dawns** (圆皎洁),
How shall I **speak before all** (人前教我怎生说)?
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.

**Pure and clear water** (净清水),
**Lingering snow’s brilliance** (玲珑雪),
Their **radiant interplay** (交光朗照) **reveals the bright and discerning** (知明喆).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.

**Pounding the elixir** (捣练子),
**Truly refined** (真了了),
In **leisurely ease** (闲行闲坐), **let the Dao’s call resound** (任歌叫).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.

I **know this well** (我咱知),
**Others find it hard to grasp** (人难晓),
For **within the curves lies the Threefold Radiance** (曲中有个三光照).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.

**Moon at the pool’s depths** (潭底月),
**Frost within the snow** (雪中霜),
Those who **truly comprehend** (有人会得) **are swept by Dao’s wild gusts** (便风狂).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.

**Gathering from the spring’s source** (泉底拢),
**Gold within the water** (水中金),
With **tips of refinement** (尖竿尖上), **search the subtle essence** (细搜寻).
*Lai li* □, *li lai* □.

**Picking fragrant verdure** (搜芳翠),
**Laughing at its lightness** (哂轻盈),
At **dusk, suddenly hearing the voice of selling flowers** (暮然听得卖花声).

**Brightest Yang Day** (艳阳天),
**Qi and climate clear** (气侯明).
**Morning clouds white** (朝云白),
**Evening breezes pure** (晚风清),
**Hiding and revealing the Essence of the Jade Petals** (遮藏吹转蕊珠精).
**Spreading fragrant aroma** (放馨香),
**Filling the tree with splendor** (满树荣).
**Dotting the Vermilion Peony** (点绛历),
**Pity the delicate child** (可惜娇儿),
**Awakened, nimble, and bright** (惺惺伶俐聪明作).

**Soul’s Platform** (灵台廓),
**Round and luminous** (圆明光烁).
I **pledge to meet at Penglai** (我许蓬莱约).
**Sever the hempen cord** (断却麻绳),
**Now it is time to refine the elixir** (正好修丹药).
**Today, instead, I buy a copper rope** (如今却，买条铜索),
**To bind the feet that tread the clouds** (缚住踏云脚).
