**A Gift to a Friend**
**Your form and bearing** (观公形貌),
**Vibrant and bright** (青春伶俐真惺洒).
**Naturally refined and elegant** (偏幽雅，自然婴姹),
**Do not let the wild one play** (莫放猿儿耍).
**Recognize the clarity of leisure** (认取清闲),
**For future tales of joy** (异日成嘉话).
**As for words and phrases** (之乎者),
**Let them rest in ink** (便休书写),
**Nurturing the priceless Dao** (养就丹无价).

---

**玉洞门开深浅** (玉洞门开深浅),
**宝树花分篆香** (宝树花分篆香).
**Penglai’s isle of immortals is my homeland** (蓬莱仙岛是吾乡),
**After the feast, the Hall of Jade** (宴罢后琼堂).

---

**Attendant of Fragrant Incense** (侍香金童),
**The Dao’s cultivation** (大道修持),
**All things fade away** (物物俱尽悔).
**Do not stir the black smoke** (莫起黑烟生叆叇).
**Clouds and waters must be pure** (云水净清须慷慨).
**In ease and grace** (逸优游),
**The marvelous and the strange** (做成奇骇).
**This practice refined** (垒这功行),
**Is like a mountain and the sea** (便恰如山与海).
**In seclusion, true leisure** (得阒裹、真闲诚自在),
**A crimson glow envelops the treasure array** (一块红霞笼宝排).
**Transforming into jade** (化玉成形),
**Turning into radiant light** (转生光彩).

---

**菊花新** (菊花新),
**Gazing at the moon** (对月无何添雅致),
**Green clusters, yellow blossoms** (丛绿花黄偏有异).
**Precisely on the Double Ninth** (正是遇重阳),
**Cold frost and dew** (霜露冷),
**Fitting to display auspicious signs** (宜呈祥瑞).
**Pure fragrance fills my words** (清香覆我如言志),
**When the wind harms** (害风来),
**Let it not be seen** (且休攀视).
**Together we shall reach Penglai** (应共到蓬莱),
**On the jade banquet** (琼筵上),
**Where the immortals bestow their gifts** (众仙颁赐).

---

**Woodlan Flower Order** (木兰花令),

**Crane-child, often gathered** (鹤儿每每常相聚),
**Pecking at the sparse blue moss** (点点苍苔啄食觑).
**In the empty sky, its cry pierces the heavens** (青霄空外唳天时),
**Under the moon’s light, it frequently alarms the dew** (明月光中频警露).
**In leisurely grace, its feathers fresh and clean** (逍遥鲜洁理毛护),
**In freedom, it walks with measured steps** (自在游行惟顾步).

「Delightfully summoning the dancing **qi** of the wind,
Six **immortals** follow me to the **Penglai** Isles.

**Peony** (Peony Order)
The Fourth Brother’s beard must be the **incense burner** (安炉灶),
Do not let his mind and body be in turmoil.
Luminous clarity is his innate true nature—
When **qi** is refined and nurtured, his spirit grows vibrant.

**Mercury and Lead** (汞铅) yield to each other’s essence,
Only then does one perceive the **Dao/Way** without name.
This night, who drinks wine together?
Recognize the days when **clear wind** and **bright moon** are close companions.

Again, **taking the elder sister as one’s present parents** (以嫂为见在父母),
The **King of Harmful Winds** (害风王) adheres to the **Longevity Dao/Way** (隆道).
Freedom and leisure are truly good.

Beyond sleep, he knows nothing at all—
A hundred flowers mock him for not seizing the moment’s advantage.
When virtue/power is fulfilled and practice is complete, he must depart early,
Taking the **cloud-path** (云步) back to **Penglai**.

A joyous meeting at the **Yao Pool** (瑶池),
Together plucking the **entwined peaches** (蟠桃) from the branches laden with past fruit.

**Midnight Immortal** (月中桂)
Falling upon the **Mid-Autumn Festival** (中秋),
Near the first watch, the **qi** is crisp and refreshing—
The wind stilled, the clouds dispersed.

**Vacuous void** (虚空) descends with dew,
Revealing a **clear sky** (晴天) across ten thousand leagues,
Displaying the **jade platform** (青玉案).
Lifting my gaze toward the seaside,
A **golden lotus disk** (金盘) emerges, radiant and dazzling.

Not only does every household shine,
Everyone rejoices together—
The poor and rich all vie to gaze.

Who can comprehend the **pure radiance** (清辉)?
This **silver rabbit** (银蟾) wraps its face,
Deeply concealed within **Yang’s calculations** (阳算).

Stars are sparse, lodges few,
The **magpies and crows** (鹊乌) fly away,
Taking **separation** (离) as their companion.

One full and round orb—
Right at noon, precisely half its cycle.

Ever more brilliant and resplendent,
The **nun’s courtyard** (庵前) beckons me to ascend the **Celestial Han** (冲霄汉).

**Golden Banana Leaf** (金蕉叶)
How can **entanglements of fame and gain** (名利牵缠) be thoroughly abandoned?
Who would dare to **bind all auspicious connections** (善缘总结)?
Dwelling in the **fire-house** (火宅) and often scorched,
Still entangled in the **chain of evil karma** (联恶业).

Cunning rivalry is no match for **guarding simplicity** (守拙),
Early departure from **clinging thoughts** (机心切切).
Slightly understanding the **secrets of the Three Teachings** (三教秘诀),
He is neither born nor extinguished.

**Willow Branch** (杨柳枝)
Life and death must be observed by oneself,
Carefully examined.
A blade at the neck—how painful and sour!
The most difficult trial.

Do not yet believe, but try the **needle’s test** (针略试) with caution—
Its agony is manifold.
**Generous intent** (发心) must be tempered by **awakening the heart’s chill** (觉心寒),
For that is the **far superior feast** (远佳餐).

**Scraping Drum Festival** (刮鼓社)
The **Scraping Drum Festival** (刮鼓社),
Within this **Scraping Drum feast** (刮鼓食), beats are struck.

Now the text reads:

「Yet when the **mung bean** (豌豆) emerges,
It surpasses wheat and barley in size.
It follows the five directions’ hues—
Green, red, yellow, black, and white combined,
And aligns with the five directions’ **auspicious patterns** (标格).

Steamed, stir-fried, boiled, roasted, or eaten raw,
Steamed to perfection, boiled, roasted, or eaten raw.
**Scraping Drum Festival** (刮鼓社),
Here within the **Scraping Drum feast** (刮鼓食) one may feast to fullness.

I observe the **mung bean** (豌豆) when it comes to fruition,
Its **vines** (圌) rise—then it must be stored in the **granary** (窖).
Do not harvest too much, nor begrudge a little.
Above, the **Three Lights** (三光) shine naturally—
Like chess, why laboriously strike the cannon?

As many know it as know it,
**West River Moon** (西江月)

To seek virtue for oneself,
One must first extinguish all **concerns of gain and loss** (虑思绝泯).
Reduce wealth and curb desires to nurture the **Field of the Elixir** (丹田),
And act appropriately when the opportunity arises.

The aged and young naturally have their **destinies** (禄),
So cease your endless toil and **fretful exertion** (苦苦孜煎).

Release a **lotus flower** (白花莲) into the open,
And the **West River Moon** (西江月) will surely appear.

**Master Wang Zhe** (王喆) harbors a **good Dao** (好道),
Yet **Harmful Wind** (害风) compels him to leave home.
His **entanglements** (攀缘) all vanish like clumps of sand,
Unfazed by his wife’s and children’s **curses** (咒骂).

He prefers the company of **clear wind and bright moon** (清风明月),
To **sleeping** (谕) even at the **four corners of the earth** (海角天涯).
Coming and going, he strides above the clouds,
This **effortless transcendence** (逍遥) is priceless.

**Nurturing the body** (养甲) is no match for **nurturing the mind** (养性),
**Cultivating the self** (修身) is no match for **cultivating the heart** (修心).
From beginning to now, all **effort and artifice** (做作),
Each day toiling for what?

He delves into the **subtle mysteries** (幽微),
And seeks the **profound principles** (玄理).
Let me teach you to **glimpse the gold within water** (稍悟水中金),
You shall not **waste time in desolate places** (荒郊) as such.

**Riverbank Moon** (川拨棹)

This **method of cultivation** (修行诀),
Is arranged with **order and sequence** (次节).
The ** Dao’s clear and tranquil essence** (清静天机),
Is revealed today—its **mysteries** (漏泄) made plain.
It causes all to **bloom like jade flowers** (玉花结).

From the start, each step is **steadfastly laid out** (稳铺设).
At the **first watch** (五更裹), glance and see the **array of myriad phenomena** (万象列).
The **sitting upright star** (坐正星) is sought out,
Its **internal form and disposition** (位貌) are distinct.
In the **eastern direction** (向东方), it **blooms like jade flowers** (玉花结).
Silver and **pure essence** (素) refine into **gentle heat** (细得热).
The **tortoise** (乌龟) is tightly bound.
Then its **four legs** (四只脚),
**Fierce and twisted** (狞狞), are all snapped.
**Harmful Wind** (害风儿), how does one speak of it?

At the **first watch** (一更裹), a fleeting glance,
To see the **array of myriad phenomena** (万象列).
The **sitting upright star** (坐正星) is discerned,
Its **internal form and disposition** (位貌) are **singularly unique** (偏别).
In the **eastern direction** (向东方), it **blooms like jade flowers** (玉花结).
Silver and **pure essence** (素) refine into **gentle heat** (细得热).
The **tortoise** (乌龟) is tightly bound.
Then its **four legs** (四只脚),
**Fierce and twisted** (狞狞), are all snapped.
**Harmful Wind** (害风儿), how does one speak of it?

At the **second watch** (二更裹), a fleeting glance,
To see the **endless flow of the Milky Way** (天河流无竭).
Suddenly, waves surge **bright and vast** (耿耿洪波),
Sparkling and **radiantly clear** (泼滟滟底昭彻).
In the **western direction** (向西方), it **blooms like jade flowers** (玉花结).
**Golden sprouts** (黄芽) emerge, yet not **nirvana’s** (涅) hue,
The **tip of the tortoise shell** (甲尖) strikes **white snow** (白雪).
Here is a **spirited child** (灵童),
Who waves his hand and personally snaps its legs.
**Harmful Wind** (害风儿), how does one speak of it?

At the **third watch** (三更裹), a fleeting glance,
To see the **silver hare** (银蟾) round and unbroken.
It emits a **wheel of luminous light** (一轮光明),
Filling the sky with **distinct clarity** (莹然有别).
In the **southern direction** (向南方), it **blooms like jade flowers** (玉花结).
The **white deer** (白鹿) comes forward, **stealing** (行得窃).
It **seizes its newly bright and pure** (新皎洁) essence,
And carries it to the **peak of the Gui Hills** (圭峰山头),
Alone, **gnawing softly** (啮啮) within its mouth.
**Harmful Wind** (害风儿), how does one speak of it?

At the **fourth watch** (四更裹), a fleeting glance,
To see the **Big Dipper’s** (斗) stars blazing like a furnace.

「Shining through all the void with pristine clarity,
It radiates boundless luminous *qi* (灵辉) sharp and pure.
In the **eastern direction** (向东方), it **blooms like jade flowers** (玉花结).
The **three mountain peaks** (三山) gather torches like lightning streaks.
Their brilliance dazzles like **fragments of pearl dew** (琼瑶屑).
**Awakened and discerning** (惺惺了了), all **steal in secret through the night** (中宵盗窃).
**Harmful Wind** (害风儿), how does one speak of it?

At the **fifth watch** (五更裹), a fleeting glance,
To see the **Polaris** (魁□) without defect or flaw.
It aligns perfectly with the **Heavenly Heart** (天心), **directing the cosmic order** (斡运),
Worthy to serve as **Heaven’s throat and tongue** (上天喉舌).
In the **central direction** (向中央), it **blooms like jade flowers** (玉花结).
**Seizing** (捉得) the essence of pristine clarity this time,
It **forever banishes** (永永除) the cycle of birth and death.
This **freedom and boundless ease** (自在逍遥), only I **grasp and manipulate** (拈捻).
**Harmful Wind** (害风儿), how does one speak of it?

The **verse’s meaning is complete** (曲中词彻),
And its **origin and significance** (历事) can be fully explained.
Dwelling in the **outskirts of Jingzhao Prefecture** (京兆府外县),
Amid the **lonely clouds and white snow of Zhongnan** (终南方孤云白雪).
I **observed** (观得) the **jade flower formation** (玉花结).
**Reviving the dead** (活死人), it **releases some inferior essence** (放些劣).
**Buried in the earth** (没地埋), the **true joy remains** (真欢悦).
**Dao/Way** (道) name: **Chongyang Zi** (重阳子),
Surname **Wang**, given name **Gu**, character **Zhīmíng** (字知明).
**Harmful Wind** (害风儿), how does one speak of it?

**[Title missing]** #3

The **nature** asks: *"Why must this maiden wed?"*
This **boundless youth** gallops wild—
**Radiant flesh**, ever luminous, ever bright.
Lead and mercury blend, **qi** refined,
**Divine stillness**—then heaven’s hammer strikes.
**Lord Li’s** true essence, **Lord Li’s** true essence,
**The fool** and **Ox-child**—like ink spilled black,
Dragged back, yet turns not round.
To rivers, fields, they crave the water, grass,
**Unbridled** in their wanton flow.
**Endure this restless heat**—
Whip harder, spur them on.
**Beat them senseless** till they freeze to frost.
**Drunken Moon on the River** (*Pine-Slave’s Grievance*)
**Heart unbound**, **careless ease**—
Let worms dissolve, let corpses fade.
**Serene stillness** guards the **precious vessel’s mouth**,
**Opening and closing**—though powerless to turn,
**Preserve the essence whole**.
When **three suns** meet, **five spirits** gather bright,
Yet though you sleep, you wake not—
**Nourish the face**, **pure as jade**, **countless days**.
Till **clarity** dawns, **true soul** awakens clear.
**Nature** forms the elixir—
**Round light** blazes—**Master’s grace** reveals.
**Crimson clouds** swirl—then **welcome home**.
**Plum Blossom Tune**
**Little fortune**, **early orphaned**,
**Withered**, **helpless**, **no one to confide**.
**Daily thought**, **daily thought**—
This truth is clear, **heaven knows**.
**Urgent summons**, **urgent summons**—
**Serving brings** your **blessings multiplied**.
**Filial heart**, **filial heart**—
**Move the divine**, **great blessings** follow.
**Human fate**—born in **China’s land**,
**Clothing, food** by **ancestral grace** ordained.
**Life’s lot**—**sigh**, **sigh**—
**Heaven gives poverty**, **no wealth to rest**.
Like **grass-dew**, fleeting as man’s breath,
**Morning’s keep**—**no evening’s trust**.
**Seek not force**—
**Seek not force**, though you strive,
**Grasp it hard**, it slips away.
**Follow fate**, **live content**—
**Greed and fear** are all delusion.
**Noble kin**, **wealthy neighbors**—
**Pity the lone**, **comfort the aged**,
**Take and give** as **heaven’s truth**.
**In power**, **do not oppress the weak**—
**Beware** when **fortune turns**.
**Diminish arrogance**—
**Diminish pride**, high or low,
**Equal all**, as one.
**Sūtra of the Blue Lotus** (*Holding the Cup*)
**Recognize it now**—**no need to part**.
**Deep jade caves**, **coral light** shines faint,
**Dragon coils**, **tiger winds** around the **jade flower**.
On **West River’s waters**, **crows fly past**—
Till **Green Boy** takes his post.
Then **wear the jade crown**—
**Trickery’s garb** is vain.
Only here **forever stays**.
**Ugly Slave’s Lament #4**
**A disciple asks of transformation**:
Alas, within **yin-yang’s vast design**,
**Creation’s work**—no **west or east** to speak of—
Only in **three luminaries’ refined qi**.
If you **grasp the swift footing**,
**Free as a drifting cloud**, **cast off mortal bonds**,
A **true spirit** soars into **azure sky**.

**Again** (*Kunqi Mountain*)
**Sunrise at the Mulberry Tree**—
**Penglai Island** near—
If you would **truly meet**,
**Only emptiness** will do.
**Unbounded ease** alone brings you there,
**Gazing down** on **lost souls’ shore**,
**Refined till wrapped**—
A **peaked gem** gleams on high.

**Waves Swept Sand**
**All things** press not,
**All things** have no heart.
**Essence preserved**, **qi** nurtured—**source profound**.
**Ancestors’ grief** grows deeper still,
**Monkeys, horses** tightly bound.
**Jade trees** bloom first,
**Flowers split gold**.
**Fragrant mist** drifts from **lofty peaks**.
**Ten thousand silver rays** gather—
Then **joyful music** sounds.

**Again** (*Lotus in Fire*)
**Yang-qi** pierces **heaven’s blue**—
**Endless**, **endless**.
**Earth’s gate** burns fierce as well.
From **water’s depths**, **nature’s spark**—
A **red lotus** blooms.
**Early recognize** the **spring**,
**Seize the cause**.
**Tortoise’s mouth** exhales **sacred smoke**.
**Cinnabar field** perfumes—**fresh**, **new**.

**Again** (*Selling the Form—Spoken Lines*)
**Live by truth**, **no falsehoods spun**,
Though **fortune comes**, **no boastful cry**.
**Blessings grow**, **family honored**—
Like **waves swept sand**, **deep sighs** arise.
If **court’s reach** does not touch you,
**Two masters** rejoice—**you ride the clouds**.

**Brocade Hall Spring**
**Ask of practice**—
Just **stepping through the door**—
How **begin**?
Let **joy** first **unfold within**,
Then **slowly seek**, **steadfast**, **pure**,
**Dispel desire**, **quiet the mind**.
**Playful ease**, **unbounded peace**—
**Search deep**, **record the subtle**,
**Often write**.
**Sudden awakening**—
**Serene**, **transcending** **suffering’s maze**,
This **vision**—**clear**, **original**—
**Return to source**, **light reborn**,
**Alone**, **no trace remains**.

**Tile Basin Song**
**You strike**—
**Swift**, **loud**!

**No omens, no calamities.**
Who knows whence this comes?
The outer lips have mouths to utter scriptures,
The inner void has a belly forming cause and effect.

Noble or lowly, wise or foolish—**ponder deeply**,
Each person casts one.
This **wild wind of awakening**—
**Unwilling to vie with others or oneself.**

**Dispel vexation, quench the mind’s fire.**
Day by day, **follow fate’s flow.**

**Unbounded ease in action or stillness,**
**Merit complete, virtue fulfilled—**carrying clouds aloft.

**Encased ascent at such a time—**
Only then does one know **the shell must be broken.**

---

**Hail the Sacred Reign**
In the **midwinter’s fine season**, the **spirit-child arrives**,
Reporting **yang-qi’s** first ascent.
**Golden sprouts burst forth, jade nectar waters them,**
Layer upon layer of **honored splendor**.

The **Jia-stem’s** **pure luster**, the **Geng-stem’s** **metallic hue**—
Interspersed stars **align their power**.
With **auspicious pearls**, **radiant and blessed**, they welcome **luminous light**,
Soaring beyond the clouds.

---
**Painted Night’s Music (藏头词)**
□ **Gold** separated—**do not let it err**,
□ **Years**—how does one act?
□ **Before the head**, what **sly deceit**,
□ **At the hour’s mark**, steady hands and feet.

□ **Drawn by hare-light’s fate**, **destiny’s wheel turns**,
□ **In ordinary times**, **rooted in search**.
□ **Matter bears divine power**, **clear qi leaps**.
□ **Below**, **leaning on me for support**,
□ **Scripture’s text**—**no elixir**.

□ **Heaven knows fate’s high peak**,
□ **Discourse**, **discourse**—
□ **Within**, **another layer**.

□ **The Master seeks cool relief**,
□ **At the city’s southern pavilion**, **ascending the tower**.
□ **Each finds its place**,
□ **Joy at dawn, delight at dusk**.

---
**End of *Chóngyáng Quánzhēn Jí* Volume Thirteen** #1
